ARK_battle_Dock_RCR = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {

			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {

			subtract_from_variable = {

			}
		}
		else = {

			}

			}

				}
			}

		limit = {
			check_variable = { 
				ARK_Ratio = 100
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UFA.ARK_unit_number_area_4 = 0 } 
				check_variable = { EGG.ARK_unit_number_area_4 = 0 } 
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				ARK_organisation = 10
			}
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				ARK_organisation = 15
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				css = 0
			}
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = css
				distribution = binomial
				min = 0
				max = 0.05
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				s = ARK_strength
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				a = ARK_strength
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				n = ARK_unit_number_area_4
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				m = ARK_unit_number_area_4
			}

			multiply_temp_variable = {
				s = css
			}
			multiply_temp_variable = {
				n = css
			}
			round_temp_variable = n
			set_variable = {
				ARK_casualties = n
			}
			subtract_from_temp_variable = {
				a = s
			}
			set_variable = {
				ARK_strength = a
			}

			subtract_from_temp_variable = {
				m = n
			}

			set_variable = {
				ARK_unit_number_area_4 = m
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						global.ARK_Inf_Control = 1
					}
				}
				UFA = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								check_variable = { global.ARK_Cnt_Control = 1 } 
								check_variable = { global.ARK_Med_Control = 1 }
							}
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							css = ARK_unit_number_area_4
						}
						set_variable = {
							ARK_casualties = css
						}
						set_variable = {
							ARK_unit_number_area_4 = 0
						}
						subtract_from_variable = {
							ARK_organisation = 50
						}
					}
					else = {
						subtract_from_variable = {

						}

						subtract_from_temp_variable = {
							a = s

						set_variable = {

						subtract_from_temp_variable = {
							m = n
						}
						set_variable = {
							ARK_unit_number_area_4 = m
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							e = ARK_unit_number_area_4
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								check_variable = { global.ARK_Cnt_Control = 1 }
							}
							add_to_variable = {

		multiply_temp_variable = {
			s = css
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			n = css
		}
		round_temp_variable = n
		set_variable = {
			ARK_casualties = n
		}
		
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			a = s
		}
		set_variable = {
			ARK_strength = a
		}

		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			m = n
		}
		set_variable = {
			ARK_unit_number_area_7 = m
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					global.ARK_Eclipse_Control = 2
				}
			}
			RCR = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					css = ARK_unit_number_area_7
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_casualties = css
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_unit_number_area_7 = 0
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					ARK_organisation = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			UFA = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					css = ARK_unit_number_area_7
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_casualties = css
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_unit_number_area_7 = 0
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					ARK_organisation = 50
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.ARK_Eclipse_Control = 3 }
		set_country_flag = WINNER
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { 
				ARK_Ratio < 75
			}
			check_variable = {
				ARK_Ratio > 50
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			ARK_organisation = 25
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			css = 0
		}
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = css
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0.065
			max = 0.1
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			s = ARK_strength
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			a = ARK_strength
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			n = ARK_unit_number_area_7
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			m = ARK_unit_number_area_7
		}

		multiply_temp_variable = {
			s = css
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			n = css
		}
		round_temp_variable = n
		set_variable = {
			ARK_casualties = n
		}
		
		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			a = s
		}
		set_variable = {
			ARK_strength = a
		}

		subtract_from_temp_variable = {
			m = n
		}

			ARK_unit_number_area_7 = m
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {

				}
			}
			RCR = {
				set_temp_variable = {
					css = ARK_unit_number_area_7
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_casualties = css
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_unit_number_area_7 = 0
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					ARK_organisation = 50
				}
			}
		}
		else = {

				set_temp_variable = {
					css = ARK_unit_number_area_7
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_casualties = css
				}
				set_variable = {
					ARK_unit_number_area_7 = 0
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					ARK_organisation = 50
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { global.ARK_Eclipse_Control = 3 }

		set_country_flag = WINNER
	}
	else = {
		subtract_from_variable = {
			ARK_organisation = 35
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			css = 0
		}
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = css
			distribution = binomial
			min = 0.15
			max = 0.4
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			s = ARK_strength
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			a = ARK_strength
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			n = ARK_unit_number_area_7
		}
		set_temp_variable = {
			m = ARK_unit_number_area_7
		}

		multiply_temp_variable = {
			s = css
		}
		multiply_temp_variable = {
			n = css
		}
		round_temp_variable = n
		set_variable = {
			ARK_casualties = n
		}

					n = ARK_unit_number_area_7
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					m = ARK_unit_number_area_7

				}

				randomize_temp_variable = {
